# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="22794-105">Membros obsoletos no .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="22794-105">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="22794-106">Este artigo lista os membros de tipo que estão obsoletos no .NET Framework 4,5 e versões posteriores.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="22794-106">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="22794-107">Membros de tipo são agrupados por assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="22794-107">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="22794-108">Este artigo não lista os membros de tipos obsoletos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="22794-108">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="22794-109">Para obter uma lista de tipos obsoletos, consulte [tipos obsoletos](obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="22794-109">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>
